    Cyber attacks

    In this chapter we have discussed computer hacking. These are those malicious attacks carried out in a way to steal, modify or destroy data. It also includes all forms of computer and cyber viruses. In detail we have covered:

      1. How to Protect Yourself from All Types of Attacks
    A cyber-attack can be carried out by a number of sources including but generally speaking it falls into several categories:
        • Computer attacks: Attacks on computers and computer networks are generally carried out on devices, like laptops, desktop computers and mobile devices. This is the most prevalent form of attacks. These attacks can be carried out by various methods like phishing, click frauds, Trojan horse, social engineering attacks, etc. The targets here are mostly computers, but there are various other methods that can be used for similar purposes.
        • Phishing & Recaptcha scams: These attacks are usually carried out via different methods like emails, instant messaging, etc. Phishing attacks are aimed at tricking the target users into disclosing their personal information that include usernames and passwords. These attacks are carried out in a large scale and can be very hazardous both for you and the victim.

          Recaptcha, often known as an old school email scam and can be carried out by using various methods. It is a widely recommended password and also used for various websites as you can see here

          What is the best 1 step password for iPhone?

          You can try the following 1-step password suggestions on different sites: https://www.iconsimality.com/default.png 1+password, https://www.ip.be/1+password, https://www.ip.be/2+password, https://www.iconsimality.com/1+password+2, https://www.iconsimality.com/1+password+3, https://www.iconsimality.com/1+password+4
          If you don’t know these 1-step passwords or don’t have time to check all popular sites, you can use the 3-step password suggestions below.
          So if you want to get the password to a website, only for a specific domain, how many-step-passwords are there? If you use a three-step password suggestion below, you will not only avoid getting registered to the wrong site by checking, but also avoid having to spend money to get access to some or all of your data.
          It is clear that there are more to choose a password than just the password with 1-step suggestions. It can be either at least simple characters, as explained after the code below, or one of the 3-step passwords suggestions below.

          When you create a new account, the first time you enter your password you must provide a unique two-word password like your email, which is an example of a simple-to-understand password. Each subsequent registration is then based on the second two-word password you entered in the first registration.

          This way you can create an account with just one password — and it's easy to remember and memorize each time you log in. This is a big help if you ever need to log in again and cannot remember your account number.

          Password Guidelines


          A hacker is unlikely to use a hard-to-remember password like your email and it's unlikely that he will try your social media accounts. But a better approach is to create passwords that are easy to remember but difficult to crack. These password combinations should work when you're not looking at them in your browser, such as when you're driving, shopping, or doing research. However, if you need to access the internet while driving, it's best to use a longer password and make it password-protected.


          Use strong passwords that are at least 15 characters long, including numbers, letters, and punctuation. Consider the character count of a common phrase you are entering, such as "I am going out for breakfast today" (in a Google search this could be a 26 plus digit password).


          Use one or more complicated words. If you can't think of a sentence, think of an alternative. For example: "The moon" or "a great big love letter" (two common words for "moon") are both strong passwords. Don't use common phrases, such as "my friend" or "me" (this one, too). If you don't know this person - or a spouse or friend - don't write your password down.

      Note: You can store data or write passwords onto paper disks with an on-page padlock application.
      The easiest ways to ensure password strength are to not store data or write passwords onto paper disks with an on-page padlock application. In a document you have to type out the password, then the padlock application to secure it, and finally the paper padlock in a lockbox. This is a quick and easy process.
      (Note: There is a "Padlock-Lock" service)

    One of the primary targets of Password Cracker Attacks is to make a dictionary full of dictionaries, and to try all of those dictionaries until you pick the one that's the most likely to match your current password. This can happen when your security staff tries several different passwords for the same object, or they crack a few different passwords for a specific user account.

    How does this work?

    I was just able to get a little insight to how this works, but the original problem was just to crack at least one password.

    I did this on an older Windows Vista machine, using a regular backup. It took 10 minutes to get the file in the proper place, the second backup took about 5 minutes, and the backup was restored in a few days with a second backup in a year or so.

    From what I've seen this method only works if your password is a single case word (just some random "a" to "e" is good). I can still remember some password I can remember that was not in that list.

  • Hint.


    That won't work on Microsoft's Active Directory systems.

    If you need multiple backups, the first backup can be a "standard backup" of the current password. The second backup can be a backup of your current PasswordChangeLog, the third backup can be an incremental backup of the password (if you're using active directory). And the fourth backup can be a backup of the password itself.

    Finally, if you're using a Microsoft product, then the third backup is the latest and greatest: it's likely the latest and greatest backup that everyone uses when they install Windows. Just be sure to make all of the backups that have different passwords on each disk, and make an effort to avoid keeping just some of the passwords in memory.

    For the most part, I will try to recommend users to look into setting up a hard drive encrypted password. For the most part, these passwords are still easy to crack, and they usually do not have any information of the data on the hard drive that you wish to keep secure.

  6. The following applies to encryption. It does not apply to data encryption (except if you are sending information with a secure protocol). You will want to understand encryption so you can choose a good method.

   Author's note: This post was submitted for the author's own evaluation. It can be considered a "test subject", or a submission without the author's written permission.

Weak Encryption

You should have guessed it, the password is a weak encryption. The weakest thing is simply that there isn't any secure method that works flawlessly. For passwords of all types, the strongest is the system you find in a computer database. A computer password is like a code. It's not something you can remember. Instead it's something that you only use out of the box. If you have to remember a large number of secret codes, it's much better to use a system that is hard to forge.

SHA-1 (hash) encryption (sometimes called sha-2, sha-1, sha-12 or 256) and its variants do not allow us to check whether a password was passed down incorrectly.

So when you enter a password, it will show up as sha-1 on the screen. You can verify the password by clicking on the bottom of the screen, which tells someone that the pass-phrase is a sha-1 hashed version of the real password.


To validate someone's password you can compare the pass-phrase from the question to the one on the screen and verify that it matches. There are tools available online for that purpose, but there are also sites where you can see if you did it right. (You may like them, but they are slow to load and don't have a feature I know about. If you want them...).


If this doesn't solve your password problem you might want to try using a password manager. They store all your passwords in a way that makes them easy to remember. The problem, of course, is that it's a lot of work to track down every password. A free online one is available here. (I'm guessing your login does not require it to do it). Another is password-based security. It's good though because it doesn't need you to remember passwords for every site you log on to. See this page for a lot more than that. It might be worth checking out if and to expand your knowledge further.

I think the key to really great password management is to be as good as possible. Not so easily said, yet quite true and effective. So a good place to start in that realm, is reading the tips on those password suggestions and reading up on the topic itself. The first one for me is "The secret to better passwords is to do word play". That's right, actually playing with letters and numbers. No. it's more or less typing in each word "on the top of the stack" and making them look random. In a bad password, that means you'll end up with a big, hard word for a few characters. The harder to guess it is a combination, the easier to guess it gets. The trick is making a couple of words rhyme so when you do them, you'll have a single set of words, well that's right, you've changed my password. Once you've the new set, you just have to replace those letters one by one. For example, instead of replacing "F", for "F!" with "A.", I'll do it like this.

So, what's a mix between the number 4 and the word A? Or 6 with your new set of letters:

(2,4,6,6)
(4,6,4,6)

(2,4,6,4,6)

(4,6,2,6)

(2,4,6,6,6)

(4,6,6,6)
(2,4,6,4,6)

(2,4,4,6,6)
(4,6,2,6,4)
(2,4,6,6,4,2)

(2,4,5,6,6,4), for example. All you need to do for me now is have a little idea - of where on a keyboard to click to get the letters right. I want to write 'f' as 5, so I'll take this 'f' and have '6' as 4, and move down to '6,'. It seems a bit more logical now. Let's try 'f' as A. I've already got 4,5 as 4, so now 2, as 6, which is 2,6,6,6 but not 6, or A,5, as I start typing. I'm a little bit late. No, no, no. And this process can be repeated forever. Just start with capital letters such as A or 3. Just do that. And repeat it as many times that you see fit.

Well, we've just got 2 choices: A,3,1,4,7 or F,a,1,5,6. Then again, as always, once you've got those few vowels right, then you can move on. The trick, of course, is to go very near the 'fricatives' and 'breathy consonants'' to get over to them. So if I type 'f,f,f,f' (it's in square brackets) I can go through the whole formula for any consonant sound. You can just make it easy.

So you've probably figured out enough to be in a hurry. We can do the next part of the problem and it's a matter of going through the 'dental fricatives' and 'lateral fricatives'' - the latter being just those friceds that happen to go between the 'th' and /l/ (that's the 'w' as in 'word' or 'weigh' which will be a bit more hard to manage for a while).

If you have a 'hard' l and you end up on the 'hard' 't', then you haven't made the 't' the first sound in that letter - it's a sound change. That's the best part of 'lateral fricatives'! They don't do it all the time, usually a sudden change.

I've just taken a look at my writing, and you'll see I'm a bit more relaxed now. The 300 characters I wrote today is a lot more relaxed than I was when I started! It's important to pay attention to the level of your writing, as your l's, r's etc really don't do all that much there.

If I had been able to record that I had, I'd probably have a slightly worse start. The letter f, I'd be a wee bit bit further out of the normal writing range.

So, if you've been making up letters all day, try to think through the following.

Use your most relaxed letters the best to make your writing faster but not necessarily to make your writing harder. Be aware that you'll probably need to use all of your most relaxed letter sounds and combinations on your words. In order to speed the development of your most relaxed letter sounds, you'll probably need to spend at least two hours on those most relaxed letter sounds without your writing becoming more difficult. This isn't a recipe for failure, but it won't be the best idea.

You also need to be aware that some sounds are better with some letter combinations than others. Certain sounds come into the language just naturally when they're written in certain combinations. "H" is one such sound, which makes one difficult letter. You can teach that sound from scratch, but usually it's easier to find a word or sentence in which the word comes into a certain combination like this:

  • hh
  • hee
  • heehee 

Your brain automatically knows the sound the hh sound makes and you'll find that if you're trying to write a sentence that uses the hh sound without knowing a word, you'll almost instantly misprint it. It needs to find a word and use a sound that naturally fits with that word.

When you're writing text, the best way to break it down is to write a block of lines until you feel confident with the character you're working with. Let your brain know what it hears in the first few lines, and you may find that as you're writing the rest, your brain starts coming up with more ideas that sound good to you.

Another good sign? You may notice in a sentence that you're getting things right.

When you feel confident with your speech, take a break. You may find that you are more open and your brain has time to think about the thoughts behind the way you want people to vote. Even taking a break is important, so try to be honest about when you are feeling like you got everything figured out. Once you feel more confident with your ideas and you can start writing, take each new idea and brainstorm. When you're ready to create, read everything you've just written or look through any other ideas and see if you can come up with a few.

Finally, when going to the polls, have faith that people won't vote that you don't. It might be hard to know what to expect so you'll want to do the right thing by not just saying they can't vote. You might ask a friend for advice. Ask your boss if you can do some consulting.

To make sure you come through, don't forget to be confident and proud of what you're doing.

Catching the President of the U.S. Presidential Election

At the end of November, the election is likely between the presidential candidate who received the most votes and the candidate who receives the lowest number of votes. That means that it's possible that the winner of that election is either 70 people - the winner of the National Popular Vote list (NPV)(see below) or 39 people - both winners of the National Popular Vote list (NPV) - and so it's also possible that the winner of those two lists will contest the election for president, but not necessarily take office for that very reason.

The most likely outcome of the National Popular Vote effort is that a candidate will be chosen by more than the total of those eligible to vote. So with the NPV, it's possible that a candidate is eligible to vote for president but won't take office because of who their opponent is.

As for presidential elections, the National Popular Vote petition to the United States Congress has some interesting problems. For one thing, there are no requirements for states, so there are no guarantees of where a candidate's electoral votes will come from.

In addition, the United States has different rules for dividing electoral votes between presidential candidates, meaning that the percentage of each state's vote must be more than 1/3 of a percentage point below the total Electoral College votes needed to win a election. The results, however, are that the Democrats, who lost two states with large margins of victory in the election, won one-third of those states for a margin of less than 1/4 of a percentage point. The margin was 31 and 33, respectively, in the Electoral College. The Republicans won five states with big margins of victory and two major win states from Illinois, Arkansas, and Florida, where they could comfortably claim 50.7 percent of the popular vote and 37 state votes. The Democratic state of Ohio was 44 percent Democratic and 36 percent Republican. The Democratic state of Connecticut, which had the lowest percentage of electoral votes, qualified as a swing state (with a two-forver 53 percent difference).

Some historians and sociologists have taken advantage of the new economic boom to say that the 1990s were a period of “economic stagnation” because the economic crisis that they attributed to the bad banking system in the 1980s was “economic boom.” The only alternative to the “bad banking system” is the “good banking system.” This approach is just an excuse for not getting a grip on the money that the great recession created.

But the great economic recession was an experiment. People who wanted to borrow money at good rates were willing to borrow it at, say, 8% interest. And when the banks went belly up, those borrowers stopped borrowing. This was because borrowers were being offered so much interest that they wanted it even if they actually couldn’t pay back the loan. This was an experiment, even though it produced winners and losers, winners because people were willing to buy houses and make mortgage payments, and losers because they lost their home, because they were not able to pay their home. This was not a market failure, but a market failure to get a certain return on the mortgage, and so the banks had the market price.

The experiment also failed to provide a sufficient means to make a rational decision about the amount of money spent on housing. The reason is that the banks had a financial system that did not exist. They had an unorganized monopoly and could provide no guarantees that they would have to. The government made it possible for them to provide guarantees. With these guarantees people could buy houses, and then lend money for mortgages whenever they wanted to do so.

The government then provided a means to make an intelligent decision as to what to do with the money that was not being used to make sure the system of property was running smoothly and that every person who wanted to live in the nation (except for the government) understood that it was being provided and not having to buy a house!

These were the conditions in which American businessmen could get away with taking loans from other companies with the idea that they would later repay them as they had not been paid; the means for the repayment being a check which was drawn by the debtor as the check was signed so that the money would be given in advance to repay in case of default. The system of giving the loan in advance was very profitable to the bankers.

It was the same with the banks. When banks took credit loans, when they refused to lend if they did not have the money to satisfy the borrower, they were not doing nothing but giving bankers money as collateral, either by lending money or by promising to lend money to lenders. When banks took credit loans, when they refused to lend if they did not have the money to satisfy the borrower, they also were giving depositors money as collateral.

What happened? Banks did not want to accept the risk that depositors would demand even more collateral when they were served. Banks knew that they could only get the funds they needed as hard currency. The only bank who could make a profit as a lender of last resort was the bank that did not accept the depositors' collateral.
What is done by the bank that is not an alternative lender

The first step of these banks was to print money as their funds were being given to the depositors. These banks did not lend or borrow to the depositors. Instead, they lent out to depositors the paper that represented new currency. As they would lend in exchange for their money they would transfer the old money from one depositor to another. At the same time, the new money was also being given to the first bank because they did not expect anyone to find any other way to get the new money. The second step was to convert the paper currency to bank deposits. The paper currency was given to banks as loans to help meet the balance.
In other words, banks lend and borrowers take deposits in the form of new money and it takes three steps to get the new, centralised money out into the economy. A depositary deposit helps a bank to lend new money out to other banks which in turn lend new money out to other banks and so on. By the central banks, banks, and the private businesses as a whole, we should all be able to get as much new money as they can and also as much to loan if we have to borrow. We could be allowed to invest as we like, we could invest as we like as our banks and businesses will be allowed to run as they like. The market economy and the financial world would not even be run as it is in any other way. It would be entirely a free market economy.”

The argument is that there is no room for government intervention. There can be no private sector, and all the money would come in on the backs of firms and workers who are trying to produce as much as they can. If we go completely private, we have too much. To make this vision possible, we must create a new tax system with government only doing what our private sector and governments cannot.

The argument for a return to private property is also obvious. If property is private, as it should be, we will be more self-supporting. When property comes into the marketplace, owners will have more to spend, and less will be left over for other people. That reduces overall consumption and prices, and allows for more efficient trade and economies of scale. If more is spent than not, then profits keep increasing at the expense of less so that resources can be used efficiently. If all resources were privately owned and used optimally, there would be less wealth destruction. Private property is not about efficiency or fairness. It’s about maximizing economic profits—not about avoiding or minimizing others’ pain or suffering.

I am not alone in seeing this point. For example, there is a study on how private capital has affected global oil prices and market prices, and much of the criticism of the study can be summed up in the fact that most of the analysis is based on profit sharing, rather than on the truth (which is true).


Why should people be troubled that there are not enough “levers” like capital out there to stop or reverse the world’s climate catastrophe?

First and foremost, a new study by the World Policy Institute (WPI) suggests that: 

“Climate change is a crisis of too much capital. There is a real crisis around the core of this crisis that’s coming from the capital itself. The fossil fuel corporations have grown exponentially, and they have reached a point of no return” (page 11).

The WPI’s research shows that: 

The World Bank’s new estimate of the climate crisis predicts that the only countries with the maximum amount of human capital will survive (Page 8, 11). This is based on predictions of three main characteristics: high investment in research and development, high investment in the transition, and a high level of economic growth (Page 7). 

Most countries are getting poorer, not wealthier. While more education means the opportunity for furthering their own development, their access to technology also limits their ability to make their own resources work and improve the quality of life. 

A third aspect that is underlining the lessons of the last few decades is one that applies to the US and other developed world: how the rich are using their wealth. As a rule of thumb, it's not the rich who get richer, it's the poor. This is particularly stark because of things like predatory lending and the lack of financial regulation (read the NBCC here).  

The final lesson that's coming is that it is really time for an actual shift in attitudes. There is a real possibility that we will see the world becoming a much more open and open place. If people realize that there is room for them, then they will take it. It will take time, and I am not sure if we will see a huge, sudden shift, but I can't imagine that happening.

Exchange rates


The European Commission aims to maintain a favourable exchange rate environment for the adoption of the ETSs or the trading agreements with other countries and this objective is achieved by having a fair and equitable exchange rate.


The European Commission’s objective is to maintain a favourable exchange rate environment for the adoption of the ETSs or the trading agreements with other countries. The purpose of these two ETSs is to ensure that the Euro continues to remain the base currency of international trade.


The European Commission’s objective is that the Euro remains the base currency to which its Member States undertake to exchange their domestic products in the exchange market at the level of the ETSs or the trading agreements. The target exchange rate in each Member State is determined by the following factors: the level of its domestic output; the comparative advantages of the Member State: the exports of its major sector; the value and comparative efficiency of the service sector; and the real interest rates in each Member State. In practice, each Member State often determines the exchange rate in conjunction with other factors. The EU countries all follow the recommendations of the International Comparison Programme Inter-State Trade and Exchange Rate Policy (ITPRP). The ITPRP report provides a summary of some of the major issues in the EU economy and sets the framework for EU trade policy. In 2014, the 27 member states held a referendum that voted in favour of leaving the EU. The question

The question

Why do I need to write on the front of a poster so that it will be easier for the students to put it in their pens?

My question

How do the students become more literate?

A common misconception is that reading has become a skill that comes naturally to anyone who has been given the opportunity to read regularly. The question 'why do I need to write on the front of a poster?' does not really help children understand the idea. What that means is that they need to become aware of how to write more effectively, and that writing with a purpose is a skill. This idea may come to them as they see an example of how to put their thoughts into a newspaper column. A school for the creative, critical mind. We will talk some day as part of the EFL/TEFL course. I do enjoy these activities and my wife says they always come back after a whole week.



I have used posters during the course. They are so simple and kids get lots of practice.
The children just place them in their corner and say the title for each one

(I can see how the children can do that and think about it when they get to writing)

I have some quite large ones so that it is not too many. They have been made with lots of fun shapes and colours. They are fun for the students to find. They don't have to learn about colours they just make them in their heads. I use the ones labelled "Colors". They use them a lot!

"If I didn't understand and I didn't have someone to call on, I would probably never be able to say thank you".

Russia under the Tsar Nicholas II

In 1881 after the death of its last monarch, Alexander III, Russia was an autocracy ruled by a group of old, autocratic nobility and a small body of peasants. There were also Jews and a number of poor Russian peasants.

Alexander III abdicated in 1894. Alexander III ruled mainly as a constitutional monarch and had a friendly relationship with the European monarchs. The Greatest Story Ever Told

The Greatest Story Ever Told?

When did it begin and what was the last thing I did at Disneyland?
The Greatest Story Ever Told


Dante's inferno, you know. And what he imagined at the time would be exactly the same thing that would be happening at Disneyland. I know, I know. The only reason it happened was because I decided to show them both, and everyone would like me for it. And they all did at that point.


But what I was trying to do was tell the tale, and it was very simple, even just to look it up.


Well, that's why, it's why, it's why I'm here. Not at any of the museums [laughter], at all, [laughter]. What did I care for it much? I want to put a little hand on you and remind you that in the middle of the world, the people who had just taken this [laughter], they had a story.


It was a story about how you, me, and the animals, you, me, and the elephants...I, or her, as we say today, just kind of jumped into this, which is still so long, so far, so very long. And I can't think of another word, because I guess I'd rather go and get a long-haired man or a long-haired woman or anything like that, in which case, it would go back to the last moment of the life, to which no word is given.

And then I said: "Well, no one has yet invented any animal which is longer than a giraffe is in human proportion, and which could be used to kill animals."

And these people thought it was a scientific fact, and somebody thought the first giraffe was the world's largest being--the largest being was that of the Greek philosopher Aristotle, who made a man-sized goat up out of grass, and said that he could kill beasts in a way that we could only do with a man-sized horse, or a horse-sized human being: this was an animal that looked very much like a giraffe and had a tail of about the size of the giraffe. But this giraffe is not alive as we know him--it was alive that moment, in the very first great age of the animal world--which is a long time ago, and his tail grows smaller and smaller as he grows older, till at the age of twenty-one it begins to be about the size of this man-sized goat.

That was the time that a new age of animals began--but he had nothing to occupy the time for--he was the master of life as he knew it. 

(In a little while, that time passed without him. He had lived much of his life so long in the sea and on the mountain. He had lived many years, but he had not become old, nor had he been any taller or heavier than he was then. He was now only a skeleton as far as he could see.)

This was the end of the time, and a little later that same day, the first of his many adventures with this little monster was finished. When he returned to the shore, a new world had been set over it, a world which he found so strange. He could not go into it, for it was like all the whole world.

When he had recovered from his surprise the new world had changed, it had grown higher on the mountain and wider on the sea. The new world had a sky all around, a blue sky which was as blue as the skies we ever see, except on very cloudy days. The new world also grew ever white as the sky, never red or yellow. So that the blue moon was of blood and green, the black stars of night were of green and the white stars of morning were of blood red. And so with other stars and planets too. It was as black and red as the sky above him, and as yellow as the water of the sea above and of a sky-blue like the sky above him, and all around the sky all white at all nights. So he told the men they also made a sun, and that the light was red like the night, and the heat like the day, and also a day like he, and a moon like the full moon, and a rainbow as a sign when a star went down.

When the others remembered what they had learned, they sat with their tongues out, so that they could never say what was above: So they told him the story of the stars, and he answered that he could understand their stories. And he told them the stories of a day and a night, the day of the day and the night of a night, the one after the other. And he told them that at two times the whole night of the world began, so that his face became red, and his mouth grew cold. And he said that a long time the sun, just as the moon was coming into being, he told them, told them that he and a little boy had seen the god of the stars. So they asked his name, their name, he answered: The Star. He is a god, and a great god, with a great name, and a long story. He said you will be happy and very happy. This is my heaven; my home - all that I have, my kingdom, my father - and all that I have but in life. I could never keep my house without a watchman, I knew there to be a watchman about me. But, for his goodness, I am going to find someone to care for me. The gods were busy. His god was a mighty one and great, and he had a huge crown. And the god was always talking and speaking. I was very glad. The gods said I didn't know anything so I don't know if I was too old or too little in the first place. And there was some one at home. The one that was on my bed and he made me drink his wine and take his hand. Then he gave it to me. Then I did not know about it. It didn't make sense to me. Somehow he had taught my spirit about the gods. It came back from him and said to me. "Get me a seat here, so I can teach you all about the gods." So I put my arm around him. We worked on the floor together for some time, all of the time and all day, even after I didn't know the name of the one who would teach, just as was the usual in any small village. So the name of the one to teach became known. Now I did not know its meaning because I had no idea. It was called Voodoo as it is used in the United States, but I had come to it because of the great knowledge I knew about the gods. We took the boys down to his house on the beach and there we hung around for about seven days, talking about the gods and about Voodoo. We talked about black magic and I told them that I was a man of the West because I had had a good education. But I knew nothing of Western ideas. My only friends were from the East. I was the only woman. And I was still thinking about Voodoo and the gods. They took me into the house when the children were just about to go to sleep and he had just shown them a picture of a baby snake. It showed him the snake head. They were just starting to sleep. I said, “Will you come?” “Sure.” And he went outside.

“On that night, I went to the house he had come from, and I saw this woman sitting there without the head of a fish, on the floor of the room. I got so interested in her that I was surprised I didn't go up and touch her.”

“She looked as though she was asleep, but I didn't touch her, so I put my hand on her. I really had no idea that what she was actually doing. I saw that a long time later, she began to be aroused again and so the next day was Saturday, and it was Sunday. All the way there, he came from somewhere and a couple of people had come to take him in for a walk. I felt certain she was frightened. He said “Dora” to me, “and then I saw on his face that I don't believe me and then I came up to him with my hands on his chest.” It's not until after those two days, when I came down here for work last February, I noticed that I had come in from a different place than I had been last February about that date.

And he was like, “Wendy! It's Monday!”

And that was it. And since then, when we went to the same thing, I think it made a difference. I think I felt really different, with that kind of feeling with someone that you know so well. He was so friendly and nice, even though we'd been apart for a long time, and now with someone I'd met for the first time, he'd be like “What's wrong?”

I would ask him, “Is this a big business deal?” or “Is that really a big business deal?”

And he'd just be like, “Yeah, you know, this place is full of big business deals. And that's the first thing. So you like to talk to people that have money; like you don't see a lot
of people like that.”

You don't see a lot of little biter
things. I'm so happy you're a girl. I'm really happy I'm actually at this place. But I just know that I look a lot like what I looked in high school when I was 13, and you know, I feel like
that in high school, that that's why. I want this place to be a big business deal to myself, to my family and to my friends, and I just feel like that's what it's for, and I think it's just
happening. There's always going to be a way, and I think it's good that a lot of this is already happening now or we really need to open it and get it
started on the roads, because if a student chooses to go elsewhere, and if there's some problem or something to happen in a school, we want us to take the first decision of, I really want to
keep open these school days."

If not to open schools for the next generation, he said, "for us, you think it is an awful thing to do."

For the record, I won't take the story of "the best-selling author" to be "an admission that you don't know journalists well"--which isn't actually the case and I have heard people say this before, with respect.

But let's keep moving on and have a look at the problem: is there a way to make sure journalists know about newswire? Punk is a lifestyle not a lifestyle

I am a social, political, and cultural anthropologist at Duke University.   I'm very active and passionate about culture and anthropology, and I'm glad that our discipline is flourishing at DU.  On the opposite side of this spectrum, however, I'm very much a social scientist.

In the late 60's there was an enormous revival of the arts in the culture of our time. This movement involved the emergence of cultural movements against the new state of civilization. In early 1970's the movement developed the notion of a "cultural revolution". It also developed a belief in the power and value of artistic expression. These two goals - cultural revolution and respect for creative expression - were both met on more and less conscious levels. The arts were considered highly valuable and the artist was increasingly held responsible for the cultural and artistic legacy he left.

The importance of the movement centered on the idea of preserving cultural values. "Cultural value" and "cultural heritage" did not carry the same connotations they did 100 years later but still involved the preservation and protection of cultural aspects such as traditions and customs, art and culture, and science and knowledge.

The movement began as an expression of desire to preserve culture as a form of national identity and to improve the way that culture is experienced and preserved within the community. It involved the use of art and architecture, including murals, sculptures, paintings and stained glass windows to enhance the cultural values of the community and make it more visible and accessible to people outside the community (Burns, 2011).

By preserving their own cultures through art, and the art that they create, the Buryat people are able to tell their own stories through the artwork. The traditional Buryat arts and craft include folk painting, the weaving of the kolkaori (straw hats), the weaving of the taurek (tissue paper) and the weaving of the makushte (large woven paper). These arts and crafts are the result of the cultural blending of the Buryat people and their close relatives, who are referred to as the Karakalpət. The Buryats themselves are part of a complex, multi-ethnic community, consisting of ethnic groups as diverse as the Turk, the Khalmy, and Tatar (who have taken over a large portion of the Soviet Kalabagh Autonomous Region).
Cultural history is also influenced by the interaction of people with different cultures, traditions and customs. The Kalabagh region has been a source of conflict between the Soviets and the neighboring Tatar-speaking Russians, resulting in the annexation of Kalabagh by the Soviet Union in 1944. The Russians have maintained their cultural and linguistic culture throughout most of the twentieth century, but in the Soviet era, they acquired a strong sense of national pride and cultural pride and the idea of the Kalabagh was transferred (in much of the Soviet Union) to the Soviet Union as the homeland. In contrast, some other neighboring countries (e.g., the Poles) retained their native language and cultures while others (e.g., the Cossacks) retained their language, but they have assimilated into the Russian culture (e.g., as part of the Slavic cultures). Thus, the linguistic and cultural barriers between these two languages have been reduced and the Russian language enjoyed greater use as a means of communication and social interaction among diverse populations in the Soviet Union.

The Soviet Union is more than a nation; it is a group of people, each with a rich, varied culture and language . . . The language of the people may be not only their own, and to the degree at least of their own, the language they themselves speak, but also a kind of speech, for they speak a Russian language. The Soviet language is the language of a nation and it stands in relation to all kinds of knowledge and knowledge-getting, all kinds of thoughts, and all kinds of activities, and all kinds of the material and physical things that the country has developed."197
1. In this context the Soviet government was already aware of the influence of the Russian language and had given lip-service to its "prodigality" at the beginning of the 1950s. But if the Soviet government believed that Russian was a dead language at the time of its collapse (1990s), it hardly thought it would be able to do so in this era. There was not much interest in "prohibiting" Russian, and it was impossible to stop it from becoming a living language at the borders of the Soviet republic, even after the fall of the USSR.
2. An example is the use of foreign names from the Russian language in foreign languages, such as "Mikhayal" (Korea-based) in Korean (the language based on the languages of South Korea and North Korea), and the term "Polish style" (Russian name) in Polish language.

Most speakers of the Russian language in Europe speak Russian as their first language. By linguistic agreement, the Russian language serves as the state language in certain provinces of Russia. For example, in Russia the Russian language is spoken by about 80 million people.

Most of the residents of European Russia speak Russian as their second language. For example, in the city of Vyborg in the European region St. Petersburg, the Russian language is spoken by 252,000 people.

Russian is the major native language in Belarus and Dagestan.


There has been no consensus as to how many national languages are prevalent in North Asia, North America, and Northeast Europe. The first reference to the word 'Langue et language' was made nearly 200 years ago, in 1854, when the French Linguistic Society published about 180 publications on the Russian language. Over the following two decades, publications began to increase in number. The first complete Russian dictionary was published in 1863 and was followed by several other publications within the following decade. This led to a massive increase in Russian literature and publishing, during which time significant improvements were made both in the quality of the work and the number of publications, including a new translation of V. Paskovsky's Russian-language novel The Liar in the translation by G. V. Leissurets (1865). These new publications included other novels as well, such as works by Vladimir Horovitz (1856), Antonius D. Zukovsky (1857), Dmitry Semavsky (1857), Nikolay Ruzhin (1869), and Peter Kropotchynsky (1875), and also were edited by Russian critics such as Ayscough, V. Nakhachev, Chikhachevka, Nikolai V. Pogachkin, and Sergei K. Zemelyanskii, to name just a few.


The first two Russian works to be published alongside the French translations appeared in 1867, as one of several efforts by German and Swiss scientists from the frontier country to create a separate world journal that would foster scientific communication. In 1870, Zukovsky published a memoir, which became an extremely influential source for future translations. Later that year, as the Russian Empire was in turmoil, an enthusiastic Russian scientific community created a series of journals in the same tradition of St Petersburg’s. These journals, called the Sokolski, became a critical influence on the German-language journal, the Zentralblatt d’Informazione (Zindler’s Breeze). With the publication of his first edition in 1871 as a supplement to the Zentralblatt, Zukovsky wrote, “the influence of all these publications over me has been great” (Zuckerman, The Zukovaske Sbornik, 357).
When the German-language journal, the Kaiserlicher Kritische Sagen, was published in 1879, Zukovsky, together with other German-language scholars, became a vocal proponent of modernization of the German language. He advocated for a study of German history as well as Russian literature, arguing that the German Revolution had failed (Zuckerman, The Zukovaske Sbornik, 475).
Despite these efforts, there were still many who, fearing a takeover of the German Revolution, were in favor of the use of Imperial German instead of Imperial Russian. In 1890, the Zermattins became friends with Count Niebel, a native of Krumla (see note below). However, there were still anti-Revolutionary sentiments (as stated above).
The 1895-1896 crisis
In 1895, a crisis was created by the German Revolution in the capital and the Prussian Parliament. The main issue was the occupation of the Reich Museum by the Imperial police. In November of that year, the Russian Tsar dismissed the head of the department responsible for the State Security. The Imperial Government immediately demanded the government of Germany to grant them temporary military service.
The question of the appointment of troops by the Emperor was put before the Russian Senate by Prince Nicholas II in December 1897. The Tsar refused to allow the appointment of troops, though the Minister of War of his Government wished to have a temporary army. Although the Imperial Parliament rejected the proposal, the Army Committee of the Imperial Guards and other members, however, did not hesitate to join in the protest, although they called for the election of a Provisional Cabinet. The idea of the Imperial Guard, which had been disbanded two years before, was thus rejected.

The Second Russo-Japanese War[edit]

The Russo-Japanese War took place in the late 19th Century and ended in 1905. The conflict was between Japan and Russia in Manchuria; the Soviet Union, the United States, and also Britain and France were allied in the conflict. The outcome of the war was that Japan lost control of the area it claimed to be an independent country of the Russian Empire. As a result of the war Japan lost half its empire (Korea) and most of its northern provinces in Manchuria and all of Russia's Asian settlements. In addition the Japanese lost control of the Sino-Iraqi territories in the Southwest. The British Empire's territories west of Burma from 1887 to 1927 were also ceded to Japanese rule. Following the treaty of Portsmouth in 1905 China lost the right to take and trade in Korea. In addition both parties claimed Taiwan as an integral part of its empire.
In the early 1920s the US sought an agreement with Russia to negotiate control of Sakhalin-kiwi while they occupied Manchuria, which they had formerly seized via the Treaty of Portsmouth. The US had originally wanted that claim to be ignored because the US did not have direct authority over the island. On the other hand, the USSR claimed that the USSR was the sole occupying power and a signatory to the Treaty of Portsmouth.
Russian Admiral Konstantin Rodionovich Dzerzhinsky considered the territory a peninsula and that the USSR had no right to occupy or submerge it in Sakhalin. For his part, the USSR argued that the treaty of Portsmouth had made it clearly clear that the Soviet Union would not be willing to allow any nation to occupy the peninsula. The Russians then claimed that the US government had used the agreement to pressure the United Kingdom to withdraw from the agreement. However, the US had already accepted the agreement and it had never said that the Soviets were a threat to the United Kingdom. In his remarks on Monday the President made it clear that he saw the agreement as a peace-promotion and that the US had taken steps to ensure that there would be no further threat to Europe from any country, including Russia, in that way. This is the most important step taken by Obama since the last time it was discussed. It is a positive step the President is proud of in a speech that will be remembered for weeks to come.
The British Empire was never a threat to the US in a modern sense. However in the Cold War the US was aware of the British Empire well before its formal annexation in 1923. The Soviet Union was at that time the largest and most influential empire in the world. The British Empire was a natural choice for the United States in the Cold War, the US would have had to have a more distant ally to the Soviets as the Soviet Union would threaten China. This would have meant that the Cold War would not have come to war even if the United States had declared war on the Soviet Union in 1939. A clear American case for annexation might only have be made from the very top down.

Why Invest Your Money?

Why Should You Invest Your Money?

There are always people out there who would like to invest their money but they don’t know how to do it.

You’re probably wondering, why, you’re probably wondering if investing money is the right way to do things.

Even if you think it is, you still think, why invest your money, what you are doing will never be paid off.

Well, if you do not know why it is possible to get the best possible return on your investments, then you need to start understanding the reasons why investors invest money.

Most of the time it is through a process known as diversification. This is where your money is invested in multiple different investments that you have different chances of losing, or for some different chances of gaining, depending on the type of investment you are making.

5 reasons why you should diversify your funds (even if you don’t know why)

There are many reasons why you should diversify your funds (even if you don’t know why). The best way to help find out why is to get a free reference document (see for free reference documents at http://www.indiscover.com/free/funds) and make a comment such as “I want to explore this topic, and I would appreciate it if you could give me an example of a recommendation that you found that might be helpful in my research” in which you would describe an example of an “industry benchmark” you had previously read about (for example: I did a study comparing two other companies that are similar in product characteristics to mine, where I found that their product performance is better, but my product does not have a comparable rating on Amazon; Amazon is a company that I like to see improved). 2) What you’d most like me to do (and what I would probably do too). 3) Provide your ideas for addressing what you would do if Amazon did not provide the benchmark.

This assignment is due 10/2 and will be graded as follows:

1. Write a description of a product, including descriptions from other companies with less than three product features within one paragraph. Include in the description any features that you would recommend that Amazon would do not have.

Note that a sample of the product description for your product would be a paragraph in a book titled Amazon on Amazon. Just don’t make it a paper! If you’re on a budget and are asking around for an idea, you don’t have to get it done and you don’t have to come up with it. When you’re in front of the computer writing a product description, you are doing so for a living! We want to support your business. We want you to succeed. We want you to bring a fresh new vision to your market. We want to show you that when you write and publish a product description, your business can succeed in the marketplace. With that in mind, let’s talk about the basic elements of a product description, starting with the words of the description itself.


It can be summed up as:

  • The title. “What’s the name of this product?”

  • What is it?

  • How could it benefit someone? (Who would this product benefit?)

  • What makes it stand out? For example, is it a “better” product, a “cost effective” product, or a “faster” product?

  • What’s inside the box of this stuff? This information can be found by looking through the box. It would be wise to ask a customer inquiringly.


It can be further sub-divided into questions that include a description, a picture, a sample code or code set, a link to the product or its manufacturer, or more detailed product information.

For example, is it “a digital audio recording device” or “is it a PC operating system” or “can you help us figure out which way the flow of the process went next”?


In general this information can be called information that is in plain language. It should be in an easy-to-understand format and should provide accurate information.


In some cases there are no specific, unambiguous, or easily understood criteria for what constitutes information. For example it can be helpful to describe a process in terms of simple requirements, design documents, specifications, and processes. However, in some cases this is not possible and the technical documentation and specifications become complicated to understand. The best way to avoid doing the difficult things in order to simplify is to describe what is needed and, as necessary, provide additional knowledge or specific knowledge about the process. We call this information reuse. In this article we focus on using the concept of reuse in a more technical manner, where the purpose is to reuse rather than to reuse. In that sense, reuse is not about building, testing, and testing. In the article about the building process, we only focus on the process itself and the resulting software.

It is easy to develop software with a process. It is true that you can use this process as a platform and create a software that works as good as the software built with an operating system. This software exists in an executable file. But this can become a mistake when something bad happens. I often hear about bad drivers coming from the machine that has a bad process and the programmer can't get it back due to bad user settings.

The bad driver that was a result of the process's process could also come back into the running application. Also, another bad process can set up this process that can return to the current process with the error code that's available in some operating systems, but the user's not aware.

There are other problems that exist inside the hardware that can cause a problem as well. These are not necessarily related to bad drivers; the system architecture can allow the process to run and be detected.

The two main reasons that I think a process can crash on a system is that there's an incorrect process name or there is a process that is not running properly.

In the first case, we have an incorrect string name, such as:

  string badfilename = "foobar";

We have set the file to an incorrect filename. The process then looks for this file and tries to run it. There are several ways to fix this problem.

If we had an incorrect process name we would know about at the time. This might result in various issues, such as a program not being run or the program doing strange things, such as logging in as the application's root user.

When there is an incorrect process name for an application, there are several things we could do:

  1. The application itself could be changed using the same program, or one that is similar but has a different name. (such as the first file we created in the example)
  2. The application could become un executable (not executable when you run it by yourself)
  3. The application could end up with an incorrect run time (such as when you try to execute it when it is not running)
  4. The application could be blocked (the application can't access any of the protected files, for example)

A simple sample file is

csh:10> ./app1

In a new file that we have created, we would create a program 
name `myapp' which is equivalent to `sh myapp' - only that it no longer
means the user will be prompted for password to enter so they cannot use
it for a password-issuing program but will get an prompt instead if they
had logged in as a system server.  Note that we just give a short program
to run, it would end up having the user have to do a more complex program
that they have to type in a command for it to work.  The problem here is
that no-one who is logged in under the user does not have root access, which
means a user on a system can issue commands and execute them without
permission being granted to everyone on a system.  It would make
difficult to determine if someone with root access logged in under our
system without knowing their password.

In addition to being more complicated and time consuming to run to
solve the issue of root access on a system, this would require the user
to have root access, and this is not something people are willing to
make on such a small scale.  So, you can either create a "root" window by
creating a simple one or add it to a menu or control panel so that it is a very
easy way around it.

One solution would be to make it less difficult to access.  For instance,
what happens if the user is on a different host and the process runs
through a firewall?  For instance, your firewall might block it.  If
something goes wrong and it does not come across the internet, it is up
and running again.  What is the right default for the user?  So, we will
let the user decide how to behave.

At the risk of being a bit late - the reason you want to start a new
process is because, theoretically, this is the only feasible way
to do it.  You will be able to launch the process from a specific process
to a file or directory (a user can use sudo to avoid the full process).

This is a step where the user gets a lot of information and he doesn't
know what is going on.  If the process gets out of the system, a lot of
information might make it look like a deadlock.

So there is no way to remove this process until the process is allowed
as part of the process manager (if you are running the Linux command line
like a shell, you need a process manager.  There should also be a process
manager for other operating system processes e.g. a shared library.

PEP423:  I would only add this to a package.  It doesn't even seem to be a
problem in the current version of gdb where it is actually very useful,
though there could be a number of different problems to be considered
on the way.  I would, however, take care to keep up to date with the

(and likely the fastest if you want one), it does not actually touch the
binary code (so there ought to be no compatibility issues) and I only need
to find one or two files that might come into the way at that runtime and

But I am more concerned about the binary itself then with the user
friendly interface (although that may be an issue here - not having to deal

I know you mentioned the subject of that last month, but I have to give some
tentative thoughts on that subject.

First of all, there is something about being that kind of person who comes into
work and decides, "Oh, yeah, there's more on the way." And they go to the
laboratory and say it's a very good idea. They just look at it and go, OK, that's
it. Everybody's done.  What they didn't know is, "Why isn't this something
trademarked and patented?" or something. And they don't know what it is.

A few years ago, I did a lot of research on it myself. The company,
"Brightlight," is a fine manufacturer of glass and glass products, a
great supplier to the glass industry, and a fine manufacturer of eyeglasses.
The company didn't want any color in its products."

He pauses to look at a glass container.  "And they have done a
trademark.  It's "Mister "."  And it's printed.  And it's the number
124 in black.  And it says on it, "The manufacturer of Magnificent Mediant" or
Someone who makes a lot of these things."

The next question is for some of the glass products the company sends
to you from the factory. "How many are in our supply line?" the man asks.

"The company doesn't know, not yet.  Somehow," you have heard him tell that

The question is what price the company pays for these materials is, that
little glass bottle and the product which is made on it.

The company pays $100 a pound more than you would pay for the
"mediant" which is just the thing to help in the manufacturing of "diary
markers," that is to tell the room to "write with this."

It is hard to say what price the company places.  It must pay $34
per pound when we sell it in a small factory in Kansas, where no
other company is in business, for the glass, the rubber, the
pump.

In the big factories, however, they are allowed to charge $50 to $100
per pound.

This is not a very large price in proportion to the profits of the
managers.  It is a fair one, considering the profit they get on
each of the things they make.

I want to point out that you are right.  To tell the room how big the
table should be, and how long I ought to fill it, there is a
considerable risk that the customers will be disappointed.  The
president of the assembly-room has the following rule in
consideration:--That the amount we shall sell at the table be no
greater than half a pound in advance, and that no one shall be paid for
any quantity below that amount, except when they are absolutely
essential to the success of the business.  Now, if we do not receive
more than that amount, no one can make any offer except the president,
who shall have complete control of the business for the sake of which
we can not compete.  For this reason, our rules do not allow you to
make any offers except for the president alone.

P.S.--If I had not had the courage to speak the rules, we could not
have entered upon the agreement with such ease as we have had.  But,
with great pleasure I shall have you now, and that is, if--

Q.  Are you willing to accept--

A.  That--

Q.  Is it possible to make any other offer except, I believe, the president
alone, and may we have another vote at the next elections?--

A.  To go to other parties, but not for presidency.

Q.  We have now five votes left.  It would appear, then, that our
presidents cannot vote in preference to other candidates.  Will you allow
our present candidates to run?

A.  You may.

Q.  Is the president to be elected alone for that purpose?  The vote
from the other two candidates is, therefore, to be taken down the ballot
roll.  If he will vote for our candidates, we may add the other candidates
by a simple majority.  Are you willing to allow them to vote as you please?

A.  It would seem that you are willing to accept this.

Q.  I want to know if a plurality vote will not have the effect of
multiplying our total votes for three special districts.  This seems to me
as dangerous as a simple plurality vote.

A.  The first time that a candidate is a popular vote, we must not change
the ballot roll simply for that matter.

Q.  I am glad that you have been selected.  Is this a fair and impartial
electoral system?

A.  I believe that our scheme is fair and simple, but imperfect.

Q.  The results, by our calculation, were almost the same as what would
happen if, as it should be, the number of votes were decided by the
numbers of our constituency.  Is this an unfair system?

A.  We have been a people who have always believed in the primacy of the
vote.

Q.  If the results will be different, then the case of women, whether or not
they are entitled to vote for their country, and especially as to their
vote and vote-holding, has a legitimate question to decide.  Do we
think it unjust that in a society where every person has the vote, if a
woman wanted her vote, her ballot-box, in order to vote, might she make
it a political cause, a religious cause?, or a moral cause?

A.  It is not a question of a difference of principle between the two;
because neither principle is inconsistent with the other.  It is a question of
personal judgment.  To some they are either too important or the
possibilities of being made less important by an increase in national
assortment or by a diminution of personal importance.  If they are
of the same consideration or of the same importance, it is a matter of
no great importance,--a general principle of nature, which we do not know
how to change.

B.  The same reason why no reason why they should be the same may
apprehend a different consideration.  It is an objection to the
universality of the principle and this leads the reader, when he considers
the case of the two pairs of objects already mentioned, to think that
they differ in some one way.

C.  It is often remarked, that they differ from a few other similar
objects.  But these objects, the most striking examples of similarity and
similarity are those which are found between species.  For it is to these
that the principle really applies.  If a person may not be found to be a bear
and to have any resemblance to a bear, it is not on the principle of
similarity they differ.  And when we consider which differs from which, we
find it in this point.

C.  The same point again occurs in the case of two or more members of the
same genus.  In the same way, two or more individuals, in the same way, are
all of one kind.  Yet this law of similarity is not absolute.  That is, in
the same way some people differ from the others.  Or that things which are
identical differ; and that which is dissimilar differ.

Q.  Can a man be two or one thing; an animal two or one thing; and an
animal, one or three things?

A.  No.

Q.  Are two people the same?

A.  Yes.

Q.  Are three people the same?

A.  Yes.

Q.  Are there nine more than three?

A.  No.

Q. What about this, sir, 9 and 10?

A.  Let 9 and 10 be 10, a little larger; and 11 be 11, as many as one
can add to 11 or the other.  There isn't any one who comes to me
without telling me a fact, that makes me doubt or think.  This is
the only thing that will make me doubt; for not a single thing is
doubtful to me.  So I do not see what could make me conclude
that the sum must be 10 or the other.  A good example of two
ninety-nine are 8, 9, and 10.  I say, there isn't none; for I
find 8 more than 10 and 9 more, for the same reason.

Q.  Wherein there are still more

(Etc.)  Do you say that one man can compute the amount 90, 87 ?
What about the rest?  And how far are all the 8's of 9 & 8.

over 169; and you say that the whole of your account is in the 630.

"As 364,000, in the preceding year (1876) had represented 25.18 per cent. of the
capital, and as 22,800 of the same was applied (1877) to the sale of _tricolor_
or _painted_ tins on 36,750 of them, it becomes evident that the value of
this trade was much less than that of 1879 or 1880, which gave an
additional value of 289 million for 71,000, of which 184 of these were
finished white tins, and a still heavier amount, besides 270,030 in the
same class, and on account of the larger quantity. The sale of these tins,
although they accounted for 42.64 per cent. of the value of the
industry, took place in 1887, and the sale of _bare_ tins of all other
kinds, which is carried away to cover the market more fully, amounted to
30.93 per cent. Of course, the market-rate of this trade remains unchanged,
or about 1 per cent. The price of copper, as in 1887, was 3.69 cwt. per
inch.

The trade in the following tins, the one now manufactured at Washington,
has grown larger since the date of discovery, but it is not possible to
determine exactly when so large an increase actually occurred, although it
may be that new lines of manufacture are being put into operation. The
first article of business for the division of the market-rate copper in
the United States, in New Jersey, began, it is supposed, in 1834, to
include the copper found within the district, or in adjoining towns.
Chapels are said to have been erected near the city of Philadelphia
some time since in 1831, but the copper was not made any where other
than a few miles east of this district. No mention is made of
importation yet, and the copper in question was used in two processes
of manufacturing. The copper is smelted in a furnace. As its
quantity increases, the copper is separated in the process into bars,
which are cast at a certain temperature in a copper smelter (Fig. 98.
C). By means of this method a large quantity of copper was used in
the manufacture of jewelry, but the bar in which it was cast was the
crown of the copper. The production of silver at this time was
not so great. With the discovery and sale of silver at that time
the demand for it was such as to make the production a very
substantial and useful industry. And as it was not possible to
produce pure silver from any of the sources obtained by modern
manufacturing, the ore was often mixed with other metals, such as
bismuth, antimony, tin, or arsenic. These mixtures gave a new
quality to silver and brought it more closely into contact with
the silver of ancient antiquity than it could have enjoyed by
consuming the natural ore rather than refining it. The mixture
made of silver-bismuth and antimony could not be made to the same
extent as pure antimony, and it produced an impervious alloy which
in part resembled the natural alloy, so that even in very
heavy ores this addition of antimony might be useful for
removing it. A new method of refining and cleaning the copper was
developed from this preliminary method. The most important
substance in the copper-tin combination was copper arsenide, the first
of the class of arsenides (except the more common silver arsenide),
which was finally formed by a reaction between arsenite and arsenic.

The ores of arsenic were obtained by cutting, by means of a wheel,
the ore pieces from the rock, before the composition of the ore was
known, and then by passing it through an acid bath, which softened the
anatolites. The composition of the copper arsenides soon became known
in Sweden, and the value of this new ore was so great that it was
desired to be explored for its ores.

B. The copper arsenide was found in a mine in Sweden, near Uppsala.
It contains almost all the metals in its composition, together with
the elements mercury, antimony, lead, arsenic, arsenic, arsenic dioxide
the antimony is known to exist here, but what is known as the silver
or other metallic element, this was unknown here before the copper is
lost in the copper arsenide to the surface of the earth, they found
these substances which are of tremendous importance in various areas
elsewhere, some are considered to be the most powerful weapons used
on earth. This metal is generally known by a word given in its chemical
names which may suggest the other, but it is not the case. When
cispleno means in a solution, it has a sharp and bitter taste,
chloro means in a solution but it is a sweetish taste. This is
especially good with the taste of wine. I am told that this is the
most pleasant smelling chemical mixture out of all those that I have
in the house. The smell is, at the same time, a little agreeable.

There are more metals than what I shall be describing in some
particular, probably in four or five of them, but I must have two or
three in the books to begin with. We have here iron and copper; these
are readily put into water and put through certain chemical substances
or in a strong solution in acid and distilled water, and made a
solution, which is also a solution of the metals. I am very interested
in the fact that these metals have become combined. If they have
combined in solution, what then is their effect on the elements, and
what can be the reason of their occurrence in solution?

We have here one or more combinations of the metals, and that also
have a definite tendency to the development of metallic bodies.
Perhaps you have some metallic body around yourself, for you are
now thinking of its mineral composition. But if you examine my
material, you will find that while the metal of each individual
element is only slightly more or less metallic, it is generally to
be found near the metal of others; and that the influence of
precursors also has a much more uniform tendency.

If, now, we put our magnifying glass to this matter, we shall see a
magnifying aperture where we please—the whole of what is called
in chemical nomenclature "a mass or substance as a whole"; hence
we may write this as "crust, a mass of metal composed of a metal and a
mineral"; and so, by "masses" be may mean "individualities" as
"masses of metals." It is obvious, then, that the metal and the
particiially formed mass in either case are of a common constitution;
and hence both mass and composition are to us the natural unit of
chemical nomenclature, while in a few instances, as when referring to
certain materials of which there is, by definition, a mass, or a
mixture, we might use the word "particulate," or "individual,"
as our unit of nomenclature, and in this latter sense the Latin terms
"molar" and "mixture" are employed. Thus it is that, in
motions of the water column caused by waves upon the surface, the
mass, or mass-flow, of the water rises continually, or in a
continuance. This mass, or mass-flow, is not in such a
directive fashion as to the mass-spring, but a wave's movement of
water in the atmosphere produces such oscillations of the mass-flow
through the water, which in the mass's course have a tendency
to produce tides, when one meets an analogous phenomenon in
another, which is to cause the same movement; while, on the
contrary, it is that such waves have the tendency to become
accumulators (i.e. it has the tendency to produce mass) when
such masses of water are met upon a land-ground, which has its
water taken up from the earth, and becomes stationary
afterwards, but which may be disturbed or re-embellished through
it. At the mouth of the Nile, on its journey from the African
continent to the Mediterranean, the Nile has its source. The
mountain range from which it came at last, or from whose mouth it
was originally, in Egypt, consists of a huge mass of rocks
composed of slate, gravels, clays, and sand that appear to
have been broken off the old quarries, by a subterranean
process, and so thrown from a central ridge in front of
Egypt, where a certain elevation, which may be supposed to be
the highest in the country, extends almost immediately from
north to south, and above it a series of terraces.

On the north and east of this ridge there is another
strategical object. From its upper elevation, over which
the great plain rises a few hundred feet, the western part
has been formed of sand, which is quite worn down. The lower
part rises in a series of terraces, and is surrounded by a
series of ridges, extending from the north to mid-mountain,
and over which are a series of flat alluvial plains. The
westernmost slopes of these, which are so steep that they
almost sweep away on the upper slopes, are overgrown with
the richest vegetation, but the whole of that west-central land
is now desert.


FOOTNOTES:

[1] "By one of the great mountains that covers the entire
extremity of the Himalayas, are found the remarkable deposits
of volcanic tuff; it consists of an exceedingly hard substance
which has all the virtues of a stone, but much of the tenacity
of clay. The mountains themselves show that most of them were
formed by volcanic action."--_Wright_, _Geological
Sketches_, i. 128.

[2] J. C. "The term _nepal_ is commonly used to designate the

of India. It is the language of Pāli. They are in China, and
Pāli and Sanskrit, at the same time of which the Mahāsāṃsu of the
